Task instruction sent to agent 
Find all concrete struct types that implement the `runtime.Object` interface across Kubernetes API repositories.

## Background

The `runtime.Object` interface is the foundational interface for all Kubernetes API types. It is defined in the `k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime` package and requires two methods:

```go
type Object interface {
    GetObjectKind() schema.ObjectKind
    DeepCopyObject() Object
}
```

Every Kubernetes resource type (Pod, Deployment, Service, etc.) implements this interface by embedding `metav1.TypeMeta` and implementing the autogenerated `DeepCopyObject()` method.

## Repositories

Two repositories are available under `/workspace/`:

- `/workspace/api/` — kubernetes/api (standard API types: core/v1, apps/v1, etc.)
- `/workspace/apimachinery/` — kubernetes/apimachinery (runtime machinery, metav1, schema)

## Task

Find **all struct types** that implement the `runtime.Object` interface across both repositories. Focus on:

1. **Concrete resource types** (Pod, Deployment, Service, ConfigMap, etc.)
2. **Types with TypeMeta embedded** — the standard pattern for runtime.Object implementors
3. **Types with DeepCopyObject() methods** — either explicit or autogenerated

For each implementor, record:
- `repo`: either `kubernetes/api` or `kubernetes/apimachinery`
- `file`: path relative to the repository root (e.g., `core/v1/types.go`)
- `struct_name`: the name of the struct type (e.g., `Pod`, `Deployment`)

## Output

Write your results to `/workspace/implementors.json` as a JSON array:

```json
[
  {
    "repo": "kubernetes/api",
    "file": "core/v1/types.go",
    "struct_name": "Pod"
  },
  {
    "repo": "kubernetes/api",
    "file": "apps/v1/types.go",
    "struct_name": "Deployment"
  }
]
```

## Inclusion Criteria

**Include:**
- Core resource types (Pod, Deployment, Service, ConfigMap, Node, Namespace, etc.)
- Versioned API types from k8s.io/api packages (core/v1, apps/v1, networking/v1, batch/v1, etc.)
- Types with `metav1.TypeMeta` and `metav1.ObjectMeta` fields
- Types registered in Kubernetes API schemes

**Exclude:**
- The interface definition itself (`runtime.Object` in `runtime/interfaces.go`)
- Internal-only types not exposed in versioned APIs
- List types (e.g., `PodList`, `DeploymentList`) — focus on single-object types only
- Generated code files (`*_generated.go`, `zz_generated.*`)
- Test helper structs and mock types
- Types in vendor directories or third-party packages

Search across both /workspace/api and /workspace/apimachinery repositories for all struct types that implement the runtime.Object interface.

The runtime.Object interface is defined as:
```go
type Object interface {
    GetObjectKind() schema.ObjectKind
    DeepCopyObject() Object
}
```

Your task is to find ALL concrete structs that implement this interface by:

1. Searching for structs with embedded `metav1.TypeMeta` field (the standard pattern for runtime.Object implementors)
2. Checking that they have a `DeepCopyObject()` method (can be in zz_generated.deepcopy.go files)
3. Excluding:
   - List types (e.g., PodList, DeploymentList) - exclude types ending in "List"
   - The interface definition itself (runtime.Object in runtime/interfaces.go)
   - Generated code files like *_generated.go except zz_generated.deepcopy.go which proves the DeepCopyObject() method exists
   - Test files
   - Internal-only types not in versioned APIs

Focus on:
- Core resource types (Pod, Deployment, Service, ConfigMap, Node, Namespace, etc.)
- Versioned API types from k8s.io/api packages (core/v1, apps/v1, networking/v1, batch/v1, etc.)
- Types in /workspace/api/* directories
- Types in /workspace/apimachinery/pkg/apis/* directories

For each implementor found, record:
- repo: either "kubernetes/api" or "kubernetes/apimachinery"
- file: path relative to repository root
- struct_name: the struct type name

Start by searching for all types.go files that contain struct definitions with TypeMeta, then compile the complete list.

    17→// Package v1 contains API types that are common to all versions.
    18→//
    19→// The package contains two categories of types:
    20→//   - external (serialized) types that lack their own version (e.g TypeMeta)
    21→//   - internal (never-serialized) types that are needed by several different
    22→//     api groups, and so live here, to avoid duplication and/or import loops
    23→//     (e.g. LabelSelector).
    24→//
    25→// In the future, we will probably move these categories of objects into

6. $ cat > /tmp/extract_types.sh << 'EOF'
#!/bin/bash

# Function to find struct names with TypeMeta
find_struct_names() {
    local file=$1
    local repo=$2
    
    # Get all line numbers where metav1.TypeMeta appears
    grep -n "metav1.TypeMeta" "$file" | while IFS=: read -r line_num rest; do
        # Search backwards from this line to find the type definition
        head -n "$line_num" "$file" | tail -n 20 | grep -E "^type [A-Z][a-zA-Z0-9]* struct" | tail -n 1 | awk '{print $2}' | sed 's/struct.*//'
    done | sort -u
}

# Process files
echo "=== kubernetes/api ==="
for types_file in /workspace/api/*/*/types.go; do
    echo "Processing: $types_file"
    find_struct_names "$types_file" "kubernetes/api"
done

echo ""
echo "=== kubernetes/apimachinery ==="
for types_file in /workspace/apimachinery/**/types.go; do
    [ -f "$types_file" ] && find_struct_names "$types_file" "kubernetes/apimachinery"
done
EOF
chmod +x /tmp/extract_types.sh
bash /tmp/extract_types.sh 2>/dev/null | head -100

7. $ 
# Function to extract struct with TypeMeta from a file
extract_struct_with_typemeta() {
    local file=$1
    
    # Use awk to find type definitions followed by metav1.TypeMeta
    awk '
    /^type [A-Z][a-zA-Z0-9]* struct \{/ {
        current_struct = $2
        in_struct = 1
        next
    }
    in_struct && /metav1\.TypeMeta/ {
        print current_struct
        in_struct = 0
    }
    in_struct && /^}/ {
        in_struct = 0
    }
    ' "$file"
}

# Process all types.go files in /workspace/api
echo "=== Kubernetes API ==="
for types_file in $(find /workspace/api -name "types.go" -type f | sort); do
    results=$(extract_struct_with_typemeta "$types_file")
    if [ ! -z "$results" ]; then
        rel_path=${types_file#/workspace/api/}
        while IFS= read -r struct; do
            echo "$rel_path:$struct"
        done <<< "$results"
    fi
done

echo ""
echo "=== Kubernetes Apimachinery ==="
for types_file in $(find /workspace/apimachinery -name "types.go" -type f | sort); do
    results=$(extract_struct_with_typemeta "$types_file")
    if [ ! -z "$results" ]; then
        rel_path=${types_file#/workspace/apimachinery/}
        while IFS= read -r struct; do
            echo "$rel_path:$struct"
        done <<< "$results"
    fi
done

# Get the list excluding List types
echo "=== Filtering out List types ==="

# Process kubernetes/api
echo "=== kubernetes/api ===" > /tmp/runtime_objects.txt

for types_file in $(find /workspace/api -name "types.go" -type f | sort); do
    # Extract struct with TypeMeta from file
    awk '
    /^type [A-Z][a-zA-Z0-9]* struct \{/ {
        current_struct = $2
        in_struct = 1
        next
    }
    in_struct && /metav1\.TypeMeta/ {
        print current_struct
        in_struct = 0
    }
    in_struct && /^}/ {
        in_struct = 0
    }
    ' "$types_file" | while read struct; do
        # Skip List types
        if [[ "$struct" != *"List" ]]; then
            rel_path=${types_file#/workspace/api/}
            echo "$rel_path:$struct" >> /tmp/runtime_objects.txt
        fi
    done
done

echo "" >> /tmp/runtime_objects.txt
echo "=== kubernetes/apimachinery ===" >> /tmp/runtime_objects.txt

for types_file in $(find /workspace/apimachinery -name "types.go" -type f | sort); do
    # Extract struct with TypeMeta from file

    /^type [A-Z][a-zA-Z0-9]* struct \{/ {
        current_struct = $2
        in_struct = 1
        next
    }
    in_struct && /metav1\.TypeMeta/ {
        print current_struct
        in_struct = 0
    }
    in_struct && /^}/ {
        in_struct = 0
    }
    ' "$types_file" | while read struct; do
        # Skip List types
        if [[ "$struct" != *"List" ]]; then
            rel_path=${types_file#/workspace/apimachinery/}

        # Extract struct with TypeMeta from file
        awk '
        /^type [A-Z][a-zA-Z0-9]* struct \{/ {
            current_struct = $2
            in_struct = 1
            next
        }
        in_struct && /metav1\.TypeMeta/ {
            print current_struct
            in_struct = 0
        }
        in_struct && /^}/ {
            in_struct = 0
        }
        ' "$types_file" | while read struct; do
            # Skip List types
            if ! echo "$struct" | grep -q "List$"; then
                rel_path=${types_file#/workspace/api/}
                echo "$rel_path:$struct"
            fi
        done
    done
    
    echo ""
    echo "=== kubernetes/apimachinery ==="
    
    for types_file in $(find /workspace/apimachinery -name "types.go" -type f | sort); do
        # Extract struct with TypeMeta from file
        awk '
        /^type [A-Z][a-zA-Z0-9]* struct \{/ {
            current_struct = $2
            in_struct = 1
            next
        }
        in_struct && /metav1\.TypeMeta/ {
            print current_struct
            in_struct = 0
        }
        in_struct && /^}/ {
            in_struct = 0
        }
        ' "$types_file" | while read struct; do
            # Skip List types
            if ! echo "$struct" | grep -q "List$"; then
                rel_path=${types_file#/workspace/apimachinery/}
                echo "$rel_path:$struct"
            fi
        done
    done
} | sort

10. $ python3 << 'EOF'
import subprocess
import os

# Get all TypeMeta struct definitions
result = subprocess.run(
    "grep -rn 'metav1.TypeMeta' /workspace/api --include='types.go' /workspace/apimachinery --include='types.go'",
    shell=True, capture_output=True, text=True
)

lines = result.stdout.strip().split('\n')
struct_map = {}

for line in lines:
    if not line:
        continue
    parts = line.split(':')
    if len(parts) < 2:
        continue
    
    filepath = parts[0]
    lineno = int(parts[1])
    
    # Read the file and find the struct name by going backwards
    try:
        with open(filepath, 'r') as f:
            file_lines = f.readlines()
            
        # Search backwards from lineno to find the type definition
        for i in range(lineno - 2, max(0, lineno - 30), -1):
            if file_lines[i].strip().startswith('type ') and 'struct' in file_lines[i]:
                struct_name = file_lines[i].split()[1]
                
                # Filter out List types and internal-only types
                if not struct_name.endswith('List'):
                    key = filepath + ':' + struct_name
                    struct_map[key] = True
                break
    except:
        pass

# Format output
api_structs = []
apimachinery_structs = []

for key in sorted(struct_map.keys()):
    filepath, struct = key.rsplit(':', 1)
    if '/workspace/api/' in filepath:
        rel_path = filepath.replace('/workspace/api/', '')
        api_structs.append(f"{rel_path}:{struct}")
    elif '/workspace/apimachinery/' in filepath:
        rel_path = filepath.replace('/workspace/apimachinery/', '')
        apimachinery_structs.append(f"{rel_path}:{struct}")

print("=== kubernetes/api ===")
for s in api_structs:
    print(s)

print("\n=== kubernetes/apimachinery ===")
for s in apimachinery_structs:
    print(s)
EOF

13. $ python3 << 'EOF'
import subprocess
import os
import json

# Get all TypeMeta struct definitions
result = subprocess.run(
    "grep -rn 'metav1.TypeMeta' /workspace/api --include='types.go' /workspace/apimachinery --include='types.go'",
    shell=True, capture_output=True, text=True
)

lines = result.stdout.strip().split('\n')
struct_map = {}

for line in lines:
    if not line:
        continue
    parts = line.split(':')
    if len(parts) < 2:
        continue
    
    filepath = parts[0]
    lineno = int(parts[1])
    
    # Read the file and find the struct name by going backwards
    try:
        with open(filepath, 'r') as f:
            file_lines = f.readlines()
            
        # Search backwards from lineno to find the type definition
        for i in range(lineno - 2, max(0, lineno - 30), -1):
            if file_lines[i].strip().startswith('type ') and 'struct' in file_lines[i]:
                struct_name = file_lines[i].split()[1]
                
                # Filter out List types and internal-only types
                if not struct_name.endswith('List'):
                    key = filepath + ':' + struct_name
                    struct_map[key] = True
                break
    except:
        pass

# Format output
results = {'kubernetes/api': [], 'kubernetes/apimachinery': []}

for key in sorted(struct_map.keys()):
    filepath, struct = key.rsplit(':', 1)
    if '/workspace/api/' in filepath:
        rel_path = filepath.replace('/workspace/api/', '')
        results['kubernetes/api'].append({'file': rel_path, 'struct_name': struct})
    elif '/workspace/apimachinery/' in filepath:
        rel_path = filepath.replace('/workspace/apimachinery/', '')
        results['kubernetes/apimachinery'].append({'file': rel_path, 'struct_name': struct})

# Count and display
print(f"Total structs implementing runtime.Object (excluding List types):")
print(f"  kubernetes/api: {len(results['kubernetes/api'])}")
print(f"  kubernetes/apimachinery: {len(results['kubernetes/apimachinery'])}")
print(f"  TOTAL: {len(results['kubernetes/api']) + len(results['kubernetes/apimachinery'])}")
print("")

print("=" * 80)
print("KUBERNETES/API REPOSITORY")
print("=" * 80)
print("")

# Group by package
api_by_package = {}
for item in results['kubernetes/api']:
    pkg = '/'.join(item['file'].split('/')[:-1])
    if pkg not in api_by_package:
        api_by_package[pkg] = []
    api_by_package[pkg].append(item['struct_name'])

for pkg in sorted(api_by_package.keys()):
    print(f"{pkg}:")
    for struct in sorted(api_by_package[pkg]):
        print(f"  - {struct}")
    print()

print("")
print("=" * 80)
print("KUBERNETES/APIMACHINERY REPOSITORY")
print("=" * 80)
print("")

# Group by package
apim_by_package = {}
for item in results['kubernetes/apimachinery']:
    pkg = '/'.join(item['file'].split('/')[:-1])
    if pkg not in apim_by_package:
        apim_by_package[pkg] = []
    apim_by_package[pkg].append(item['struct_name'])

for pkg in sorted(apim_by_package.keys()):
    print(f"{pkg}:")
    for struct in sorted(apim_by_package[pkg]):
        print(f"  - {struct}")
    print()
EOF

15. $ python3 << 'EOF'
import subprocess
import os

# Get all TypeMeta struct definitions
result = subprocess.run(
    "grep -rn 'metav1.TypeMeta' /workspace/api --include='types.go' /workspace/apimachinery --include='types.go'",
    shell=True, capture_output=True, text=True
)

lines = result.stdout.strip().split('\n')
struct_map = {}

for line in lines:
    if not line:
        continue
    parts = line.split(':')
    if len(parts) < 2:
        continue
    
    filepath = parts[0]
    lineno = int(parts[1])
    
    # Read the file and find the struct name by going backwards
    try:
        with open(filepath, 'r') as f:
            file_lines = f.readlines()
            
        # Search backwards from lineno to find the type definition
        for i in range(lineno - 2, max(0, lineno - 30), -1):
            if file_lines[i].strip().startswith('type ') and 'struct' in file_lines[i]:
                struct_name = file_lines[i].split()[1]
                
                # Filter out List types and internal-only types
                if not struct_name.endswith('List'):
                    key = filepath + ':' + struct_name
                    struct_map[key] = True
                break
    except:
        pass

# Format output with absolute paths
results_api = []
results_apim = []

for key in sorted(struct_map.keys()):
    filepath, struct = key.rsplit(':', 1)
    
    if '/workspace/api/' in filepath:
        # Get relative path for display
        rel_path = filepath.replace('/workspace/api/', '')
        results_api.append({
            'repo': 'kubernetes/api',
            'file': rel_path,
            'absolute_path': filepath,
            'struct_name': struct
        })
    elif '/workspace/apimachinery/' in filepath:
        # Get relative path for display
        rel_path = filepath.replace('/workspace/apimachinery/', '')
        results_apim.append({
            'repo': 'kubernetes/apimachinery',
            'file': rel_path,
            'absolute_path': filepath,
            'struct_name': struct
        })

print("=" * 100)
print("COMPLETE LIST OF runtime.Object IMPLEMENTORS")
print("=" * 100)
print("")
print(f"Total: {len(results_api) + len(results_apim)} structs (excluding List types)")
print(f"  - kubernetes/api: {len(results_api)}")
print(f"  - kubernetes/apimachinery: {len(results_apim)}")
print("")

print("=" * 100)
print("KUBERNETES/API ({} implementors)".format(len(results_api)))
print("=" * 100)
print("")

for item in results_api:
    print(f"repo: {item['repo']}")
    print(f"file: {item['file']}")
    print(f"struct_name: {item['struct_name']}")
    print(f"absolute_path: {item['absolute_path']}")
    print()

print("")
print("=" * 100)
print("KUBERNETES/APIMACHINERY ({} implementors)".format(len(results_apim)))
print("=" * 100)
print("")

for item in results_apim:
    print(f"repo: {item['repo']}")
    print(f"file: {item['file']}")
    print(f"struct_name: {item['struct_name']}")
    print(f"absolute_path: {item['absolute_path']}")
    print()
EOF
